<span id="freeTextContainer903955976258937788">4 Stars<br/><br/>And the Cat and Bone’s Saga continues. <br/><br/>Basically Cat and Bone’s relationship is solid and the story is about them two with whatever the issues are in that book.<br/><br/>I’m okay with that. I know there’s no drama between Cat and Bones, but this story was kind of interesting. The beginning was a touch too slow, but it picked up towards the middle end.<br/><br/>There’s a ghost that is causing problems and Cat is on the case!<br/><br/>I found the ghost story line interesting and different. The ghost is a piece of work a</span>
  <span id="freeText903955976258937788" style="display:none">4 Stars<br /><br />And the Cat and Bone’s Saga continues. <br /><br />Basically Cat and Bone’s relationship is solid and the story is about them two with whatever the issues are in that book.<br /><br />I’m okay with that. I know there’s no drama between Cat and Bones, but this story was kind of interesting. The beginning was a touch too slow, but it picked up towards the middle end.<br /><br />There’s a ghost that is causing problems and Cat is on the case!<br /><br />I found the ghost story line interesting and different. The ghost is a piece of work and Cat works really hard in trying to kill him. I liked that she couldn’t hurt him because he’s a ghost and they kind of had to work around that.<br /><br />The side storyline is that Cat’s uncle is still a ghost and I didn’t like the tension between Cat and her Uncle. The new man in charge isn’t Tate anymore and the guy that is taking over is causing all problems. He’s really annoying and I have a feeling he’s going to be the focal villain in the next book. I am not looking forward to this.<br /><br />I’m trying to catch up in all the books before I get to Ian’s book and yay, I only have one more. As much as I love Cat and Bones, they are kind of boring and I need a new love storyline. <br /></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27675174-shay?shelf=2018">2018</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2050180001" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2668102205708768159">For those of you who don't know about Heinrich Kramer I suggest you look him up. You can totally hate me later. <br/><br/>In this book, Heinrich is a rather sadistic ghost who has kept his reign of female hatred going for centuries. He has found a way to take a corporeal form on All Hallows Eve to continue his infamous witch hunts. However, Cat and Bones are on the case and stand up to him in a way he can't ignore. <br/><br/>I struggled a bit with this book because of how angry I got about the circumstances in it. </span>
  <span id="freeText2668102205708768159" style="display:none">For those of you who don't know about Heinrich Kramer I suggest you look him up. You can totally hate me later. <br /><br />In this book, Heinrich is a rather sadistic ghost who has kept his reign of female hatred going for centuries. He has found a way to take a corporeal form on All Hallows Eve to continue his infamous witch hunts. However, Cat and Bones are on the case and stand up to him in a way he can't ignore. <br /><br />I struggled a bit with this book because of how angry I got about the circumstances in it. The book is still amazing. The characters are perfect in their own ways. The plot was ingenious! If you haven't started this series you should. There is a little something for everyone!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7KFTpwAN73MDDFBWducVA/BiM5ZOubR8O2Bl7ZVgG6PWhzp1u1MmG6Qn5DeBEh/cJj3UXoA0OhtgHiNcWCPpOQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9SYWhPt/4Grp2ixRiTDPIpi2EVnc7mCvytekJTaRSNHPAH9WQCEpAk7xmDB+xcX9Tun2kRJj7siRqeKU+9K6Sw==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7887471187269189346">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on </span>
  <span id="freeText7887471187269189346" style="display:none">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on the weekends. Aside from writing, Jeaniene enjoys reading, poetry, watching movies with her husband, exploring old cemeteries, spelunking and traveling – by car. Airplanes, children, and cook books frighten her.<br /><br />For information on Jeaniene's books, book trailers, deleted scenes, creature mythology, and more, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jeanienefrost.com">www.jeanienefrost.com</a><br /></span>
